<p><b>Kalidou Koulibaly</b> (born 20 June 1991) is a professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as <a href="/wiki/Centre_back" class="mw-redirect" title="Centre back">centre back</a> for <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> club <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a> and captains the <a href="/wiki/Senegal_national_football_team" title="Senegal national football team">Senegal national team</a>.
</p><p>Koulibaly began his professional club career with French team <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a> in 2010, before moving to Belgian club <a href="/wiki/K.R.C._Genk" title="K.R.C. Genk">Genk</a> in 2012, winning the <a href="/wiki/Belgian_Cup" title="Belgian Cup">Belgian Cup</a> in his first season. He joined Italian team Napoli in 2014, where he won the <a href="/wiki/Supercoppa_Italiana" title="Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> title; he also won the <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> in 2020.
</p><p>As Koulibaly was born in France to Senegalese parents, he was eligible to represent both nations at international level, and initially played for the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-20_football_team" title="France national under-20 football team">France national under-20 football team</a>. He later made his senior debut with Senegal in 2015 and was a member of the Senegal squad that took part at the <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations">2017 Africa Cup of Nations</a>. He was named to the side that represented Senegal at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> the following year, and subsequently helped his team to the final of the <a href="/wiki/2019_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2019 Africa Cup of Nations">2019 Africa Cup of Nations</a>.
</p>

<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-23"><a href="#Honours"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">Honours</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-24"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-25"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">9</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>
</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Koulibaly was born on 20 June 1991, to Senegalese parents in <a href="/wiki/Saint-Di%C3%A9-des-Vosges" title="Saint-Dié-des-Vosges">Saint-Dié-des-Vosges</a>, France.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> His father worked in a textile mill in Senegal for seven days a week and never took weekends off for five years before he saved enough money to bring his mother to France.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He grew up in <a href="/wiki/Saint-Di%C3%A9-des-Vosges" title="Saint-Dié-des-Vosges">Saint-Dié-des-Vosges</a>, France, revealing that: "When you grow up in this environment, you see everyone as your brother. We are black, white, Arab, African, Muslim, Christian, yes  but we are all French. We are all hungry, so lets go have a Turkish meal together. Or tonight, lets all go to my house and eat Senegalese food. Yes, we have differences, but we are all equal."<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly says his upbringing was "heavily influenced by the multi-cultural nature" growing up.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_BBC_Sport_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_BBC_Sport-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Koulibaly revealed that he first started playing football, saying: "All the kids were running around playing football with no shoes, and I was really upset by this, I guess. My mom says that I was begging her to go to the store and buy shoes for everybody, so I could play football with them. But my mother said, Kalidou, just take your shoes off. Go play like they do. In the end, I threw off my shoes and went to play barefoot with my cousins  and this is where my football story begins. When we got back to France, I was playing every day in the little park by our house."<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> His footballing career began with local club <a href="/wiki/SR_Saint-Di%C3%A9" title="SR Saint-Dié">SR Saint-Dié</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Contract_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Contract-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He then joined FC Metz in his first spell but when was released at fifteen, which according to the club's Academy Manager, Denis Schaeffer, Koulibaly was let go "because he was too introverted, and his level was a little below our expectations."<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Koulibaly began his career playing for his hometown club SR Saint-Dié's youth team; he spent two seasons playing for the club's team in the <a href="/wiki/Championnat_de_France_Amateur_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Championnat de France Amateur 2">Championnat de France Amateur 2</a>, before joining the youth academy of professional club <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a> on 1 July 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> While at Metz, Koulibaly helped the club's under-19 team win the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Coupe_Gambardella" title="200910 Coupe Gambardella">200910 Coupe Gambardella</a> after the team defeated <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">Sochaux</a> 54 on penalties in the <a href="/wiki/2010_Coupe_Gambardella_Final" title="2010 Coupe Gambardella Final">final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He also played for the club's amateur team in the <a href="/wiki/Championnat_de_France_Amateur" class="mw-redirect" title="Championnat de France Amateur">Championnat de France Amateur</a> appearing in 15 matches as Metz were crowned champions of the league finishing with 107 points.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Metz">Metz</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Metz">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311:_Development_and_breakthrough"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201011:_Development_and_breakthrough">201011: Development and breakthrough</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 201011: Development and breakthrough">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Prior to the start of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Ligue_2" title="201011 Ligue 2">201011 season</a>, Koulibaly signed his first professional contract agreeing to a one-year deal. He was, subsequently, promoted to the senior team by new manager <a href="/wiki/Dominique_Bijotat" title="Dominique Bijotat">Dominique Bijotat</a>. Koulibaly made his professional debut on 20 August 2010 in a league match against <a href="/wiki/Vannes_OC" title="Vannes OC">Vannes</a>. He appeared as a substitute in a 10 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Following this, Kouliably became a first team regular for the side after dispatching the place from <a href="/wiki/Nuno_Frechaut" title="Nuno Frechaut">Nuno Frechaut</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> On 15 April 2011, he scored his first goal for FC Metz, as they drew 33 against <a href="/wiki/Clermont_Foot" title="Clermont Foot">Clermont</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Koulibaly signed a threeyear contract extension with the club, keeping him until 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Contract_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Contract-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the 201011 season, he went on to make nineteen appearances and scoring once in all competitions. Reflecting on his first season at FC Metz, Manager Bijotat said of him, quoting: "Kalidou Koulibaly is perhaps the one who surprised the most people, while being the one who surprised me the least personally. I knew that it would come to him because it was already showing a good maturity. He's always in the right mood and does not catch fire, it's important to the job he's doing. He also knows how to analyze his own matches, which brings him to a certain regularity in his performances. Conversely, we thought <a href="/wiki/Yeni_Ngbakoto" title="Yeni Ngbakoto">Yeni Ngbakoto</a> was the closest to the group, but it took longer to come. He had a difficult start, between suspension and injury. It took him longer to settle on the team. His game was not settled, in this area he has progressed in recent weeks and must still win in consistency."<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201112_season">201112 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201112 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>However, at the start of the 201112 season, Koulibaly missed the first five league matches of the season, due to international commitments.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> His first appearance of the 201112 season came on 9 September 2011, coming as a substitute in the 60th minutes, in a 22 draw against <a href="/wiki/Stade_Lavallois" title="Stade Lavallois">Stade Lavallois</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> However, he served a two match suspension after being sentoff for an unprofessional conduct on <a href="/wiki/Guillaume_Moullec" title="Guillaume Moullec">Guillaume Moullec</a>, as FC Metz lost 10 on 30 September 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Koulibaly returned to the first team and then captained the side for the first time on 2 December 2011, in a 20 win over <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco" class="mw-redirect" title="AS Monaco">AS Monaco</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He continued to regain his first team place until suspension and injury, which eventually kept him out for the rest of the 201112 season.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the 201112 season, Koulibaly went on to make 23 appearances in all competitions, including 10 alongside his future international teammate <a href="/wiki/Sadio_Man%C3%A9" title="Sadio Mané">Sadio Mané</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Genk">Genk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Genk">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313:_Belgian_Cup"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201213:_Belgian_Cup">201213: Belgian Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 201213: Belgian Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Koulibaly joined Belgian club <a href="/wiki/K.R.C._Genk" title="K.R.C. Genk">Genk</a> on 29 June 2012 after agreeing a four-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Among interested parties was Anderlecht but Genk won the race to sign him.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 23 August 2012, Koulibaly made his Genk debut in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> play-off qualifying round, in which they were defeated by Swiss team <a href="/wiki/FC_Luzern" title="FC Luzern">Luzern</a> 21 in the first leg of two.<sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Since joining the club, he became a first team regular for the side, playing mostly in the centreback position.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> In a match against <a href="/wiki/Oud-Heverlee_Leuven" title="Oud-Heverlee Leuven">OH Leuven</a> on 25 November 2012, Koulibaly made a foul in the penalty box at the last minute of the game, which was successfully converted by <a href="/wiki/Ebrahima_Sawaneh" title="Ebrahima Sawaneh">Ibou</a>, as Genk drew 11.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> On 23 December 2012, Koulibaly scored his first Racing Genk goal in a 42 home defeat to <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> in which he scored a free header from a corner, to make amends for his mistake.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He later helped Genk win the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Belgian_Cup" title="201213 Belgian Cup">201213 Belgian Cup</a> after starting the whole game to beat <a href="/wiki/Cercle_Brugge_K.S.V." title="Cercle Brugge K.S.V.">Cercle Brugge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the 201213 season, Koulibaly went on to make 46 appearances and scoring once in all competitions.
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201314_season">201314 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201314 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The 201314 season saw Koulibaly began playing in the centreback position, where he continued to form a partnership with <a href="/wiki/Kara_Mbodji" title="Kara Mbodji">Kara Mbodji</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He then scored two goals in two matches between 6 October 2013 and 19 October 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly started in every match since the start of the season until he suffered a knee injury during a 20 loss against <a href="/wiki/K.S.C._Lokeren_Oost-Vlaanderen" title="K.S.C. Lokeren Oost-Vlaanderen">Lokeren</a> on 8 December 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> A month later on 19 January 2014, Koulibaly returned to the starting lineup from injury, starting the whole game, in a 10 loss against <a href="/wiki/S.V._Zulte_Waregem" title="S.V. Zulte Waregem">Zulte Waregem</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly kept his place in the first team for the rest of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> However, he missed the remaining three league matches of the season, due to his imminent transfer move to Napoli.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Koulibaly went on to make 46 appearances and scored two times in all competitions.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Napoli">Napoli</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Napoli">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315:_Debut_campaign"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201415:_Debut_campaign">201415: Debut campaign</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 201415: Debut campaign">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Koulibaly joined <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> club <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">S.S.C. Napoli</a> on 2 July 2014 on a five-year contract, for a fee around £6.5&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He made his debut on 19 August 2014 in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> play-off round qualifier, in which Napoli drew 11 with <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Napoli went on to lose the second leg 31, thus sending them out of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Koulibaly made his Serie A debut in the opening game of the season against <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>, playing the whole match as Napoli won 21.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal for the side on 24 September in a 33 draw with <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_24-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly played in every match from the start of the season, before being sent off for a second bookable offence in a 11 draw against <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> on 1 December 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2014_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2014 Supercoppa Italiana">2014 Supercoppa Italiana</a> against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in <a href="/wiki/Doha" title="Doha">Doha</a>, <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a>, on 22 December, Koulibaly scored the winning penalty in the <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">shootout</a> to secure Napoli victory.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Towards the end of the 201415 season, Koulibaly found himself placed in and out of the starting eleven for the side, as manager <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Ben%C3%ADtez" title="Rafael Benítez">Rafael Benítez</a> preferred <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_Albiol" title="Raúl Albiol">Raúl Albiol</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miguel_Britos" title="Miguel Britos">Miguel Britos</a> in the central defence positions.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> In his first season at Napoli, Koulibaly went on to make 39 appearances and scored one goal in all competitions.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg/300px-Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg" decoding="async" width="300" height="199" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg/450px-Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg/600px-Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4201" data-file-height="2782" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bar%C3%A7a_-_Napoli_-_20140806_-_33.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Koulibaly playing during the friendly match between Napoli and <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> in the summer of 2014.</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516_season">201516 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 201516 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ahead of the 201516 season, Koulibaly was linked with a move to <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> side <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>, but he eventually stayed at the club.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Koulibaly became a regular starter for Napoli under coach <a href="/wiki/Maurizio_Sarri" title="Maurizio Sarri">Maurizio Sarri</a>, and saw an improvement in his performances for the side in the number of matches.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During a 20 win over <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a> on 3 February 2016, Koulibaly was subjected to racist abuse from Lazio supporters, prompting referee <a href="/wiki/Massimiliano_Irrati" title="Massimiliano Irrati">Massimiliano Irrati</a> to suspend the match temporally; Koulibaly later reflected on this as "the first time that he really experienced any racism in football".<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> After the match, Lazio would go on to be sanctioned 50,000 by the league for these racist chants, and were ordered to play two home matches behind closed doors.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> In a follow-up match against <a href="/wiki/Carpi_F.C._1909" title="Carpi F.C. 1909">Carpi</a>, Napoli supporters wore masks of Koulibaly in support of him; he played a vital role during the game as he set up <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a> to score the only goal of the match in a Napoli victory.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The matches against Lazio and Carpi saw Napoli keep two consecutive clean sheets for the second time during the season, having previously achieved this in matches between 20 and 23 September 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly made 42 appearances in the 201516 season in all competitions.
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201617_season">201617 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 201617 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;"><a href="/wiki/File:FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_(Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019)_40.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_40.jpg/190px-FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_40.jpg" decoding="async" width="190" height="241" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_40.jpg/285px-FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_40.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_40.jpg/380px-FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_40.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1382" data-file-height="1756" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_(Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019)_40.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Koulibaly marking <a href="/wiki/FC_Red_Bull_Salzburg" title="FC Red Bull Salzburg">Red Bull Salzberg</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Takumi_Minamino" title="Takumi Minamino">Takumi Minamino</a> in a UEFA Champions League match on 23 October 2019.</div></div></div>
<p>In the 201617 season, Koulibaly continued to be a regular starter for Napoli under coach Maurizio Sarri and helped the side start the season well, earning four wins from their first six league matches.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On 19 September 2016, he signed a fiveyear contract with the club, keeping him at Napoli until 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> It was not until 15 October 2016 that Koulibaly scored his first goal of the season, in a 31 loss against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">A.S. Roma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly continued to start every match of the season, until he sustained a knee injury during a 50 win over <a href="/wiki/Cagliari_Calcio" title="Cagliari Calcio">Cagliari</a> on 11 December 2016, resulting in him being sidelined for a month.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> After spending two months away from Napoli's first team, due to both injury and international commitment, Koulibaly made his return to the starting lineup, playing the full 90 minutes, in a 20 win over Genoa on 10 February 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly regained his first team place for the side towards the end of the 201617 season.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He later scored his second goal of the season, in a 41 win over <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>, on 20 May 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> By the end of the 201617 season, Koulibaly had made 38 appearances and scored two times in all competitions.
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718_season">201718 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 201718 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the 201718 season, Koulibaly played an integral role as Napoli won their first eight matches of the Serie A campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> During this streak, he scored two goals for the side, netting against Lazio and Cagliari on 20 September and 1 October 2017 respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly then helped Napoli go on a ten match winning streak in the league between 16 December 2017 and 26 February 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> During this streak, he scored two goals for the side against <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hellas_Verona_F.C." title="Hellas Verona F.C.">Hellas Verona</a> on 16 December 2017 and 6 January 2018 respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Napoli continued to closely challenge for the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Serie_A" title="201718 Serie A">201718 Serie A</a> title. On 22 April 2018, Koulibaly scored a 90th-minute header against league leaders <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Juventus_Stadium" title="Juventus Stadium">Allianz Stadium</a> to seal a 10 win for the visitors and move Napoli within one point of Juventus with four games remaining.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> However, in their next match against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>, Koulibaly was sent off within 10 minutes for a rash foul as Napoli lost 30.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Napoli would go on to achieve a club record 91 points, but finished the season 4 points behind league winners Juventus. By the end of the 201718 season, Koulibaly had made 45 appearances and scored five times in all competitions, his highest-scoring season for the club.
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819_season">201819 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 201819 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>At the start of the 201819 season, Koulibaly signed a contract extension with Napoli, keeping him at the club until 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> He continued to be a regular starter for Napoli under coach <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a> and spoke positively about playing under him.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly helped the side win thirteen matches in the league to stay near the higher positions and challenge for the league title once again.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> He then captained Napoli for the first time in his career, helping the side beat Cagliari 10 on 16 December 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> However, on 26 December 2018, Koulibaly received two yellow cards in quick succession for a foul and for sarcastically applauding the referee and was sent off, as Napoli lost 10 to <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> at the <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a>. According to Ancelotti, Koulibaly was the target of racist chants from the Inter fans and his team asked for the match to be suspended three times. Posting on social media after the match, Koulibaly wrote, "I'm sorry about the defeat and especially to have let my brothers down. But I'm proud of the colour of my skin. To be French, Senegalese, Neapolitan, and a man."<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> Inter would go on to be sanctioned by the league for these racist chants, and was ordered to play two home matches behind closed doors.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After serving a two match suspension, Koulibaly returned to the starting lineup, playing the whole game and keeping a clean sheet, in a 20 win over <a href="/wiki/U.S._Sassuolo_Calcio" title="U.S. Sassuolo Calcio">Sassuolo Calcio</a> in the round of 16 of the Coppa Italia.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> He helped the side keep five consecutive clean sheets in the league between 26 January and 24 February 2019, including matches against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">A.C. Milan</a>, Sampdoria and <a href="/wiki/Parma_Calcio_1913" title="Parma Calcio 1913">Parma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On 12 April 2019, Koulibaly was involved in another racial incident, after reportedly suffering <a href="/wiki/Racism_in_association_football" title="Racism in association football">racist abuse</a> from an <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> fan during a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> match between the two teams.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Two days later on 14 April 2019, he scored twice for the side, in a 31 win over <a href="/wiki/A.C._ChievoVerona" title="A.C. ChievoVerona">Chievo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Napoli once again finished the season as runners-up to Juventus, with Koulibaly earning the inaugural <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Awards#List_of_winners" title="Serie A Awards">Serie A Best Defender</a> award for the season.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> By the end of the 201819 season, he had made 48 appearances and scored two goals in all competitions.
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_Coppa_Italia"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920:_Coppa_Italia">201920: Coppa Italia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 201920: Coppa Italia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 17 June 2020, Koulibaly started in the Coppa Italia Final against Juventus; Napoli won the match 42 on penalties after a goalless draw.<sup id="cite_ref-2020-CI_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2020-CI-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly has on a number of occasions talked about his desire to retire at Napoli, and that a departure would only occur due to an economic decision made by the club.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Koulibaly was born and raised in France by Senegalese parents, and was therefore eligible for both nations. He played for the French under-20 team starting in 2011 and played six times during the <a href="/wiki/2011_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2011 FIFA U-20 World Cup">FIFA U-20 World Cup</a> in Colombia.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, in early September 2015, Koulibaly changed federations and joined the <a href="/wiki/Senegal_national_football_team" title="Senegal national football team">Senegal national football team</a>, despite the interest to call him for Les Bleus from <a href="/wiki/Didier_Deschamps" title="Didier Deschamps">Didier Deschamps</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-gaffe_Deschamps_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gaffe_Deschamps-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> He later explained his decision, saying: "I don't have any regrets because I want to write the story of the future of Senegal football and I hope I'll be able to do that."<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_BBC_Sport_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_BBC_Sport-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly made his debut on 5 September 2015 in an AFCON qualifier against <a href="/wiki/Namibia_national_football_team" title="Namibia national football team">Namibia</a> in a 20 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> He was a member of the Senegal squad that took part at the <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations">2017 Africa Cup of Nations</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2018, he was named in Senegal's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Koulibaly played all three matches, as Senegal were knocked out in the group stage of the tournament after becoming the first team in <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> history to be eliminated due to fair play <a href="/wiki/Tiebreaker" title="Tiebreaker">tiebreaker</a> rules.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:305px;"><a href="/wiki/File:FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_(Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019)_75.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_75.jpg/303px-FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_75.jpg" decoding="async" width="303" height="196" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_75.jpg/455px-FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_75.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_75.jpg/606px-FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_%28Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019%29_75.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2500" data-file-height="1615" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:FC_Salzburg_gegen_SSC_Napoli_(Championsleague_3._Runde_23._Oktober_2019)_75.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Koulibaly marking <a href="/wiki/Hwang_Hee-chan" title="Hwang Hee-chan">Hwang Hee-chan</a> in a UEFA Champions League match in 2019</div></div></div>
<p>A large, aggressive, quick and physically strong yet elegant player, Koulibaly is recognised for his aerial prowess, anticipation, positioning, tackling, character, technique and passing ability as a defender. He has also been praised by pundits for his overall solidity as a player and his ability to make interceptions; however, he has also drawn criticism for giving away too many fouls. Due to his versatility, he can play both in his usual role as a <a href="/wiki/Centre-back" class="mw-redirect" title="Centre-back">central defender</a>, or as a <a href="/wiki/Full_back_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Full back (association football)">full back</a> on either the right or left flank, in both a three or four-man defence; he has even been deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>. During his time at Napoli, his ability to play the ball out from the back saw him function as a ball-playing centre-back in manager <a href="/wiki/Maurizio_Sarri" title="Maurizio Sarri">Maurizio Sarri</a>'s attacking, possession based-system.<sup id="cite_ref-swoop_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swoop-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-altezza_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-altezza-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-K2_Koulibaly_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-K2_Koulibaly-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bunker_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bunker-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-giant_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-giant-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-price_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-price-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-indecent_offer_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-indecent_offer-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-style_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-style-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Currently considered to be one of the best and most complete defenders in world football in the media,<sup id="cite_ref-giant_88-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-giant-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-indecent_offer_90-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-indecent_offer-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> his ability, playing style, tall stature, and imposing physique have earned him the nicknames <i>K2</i><sup id="cite_ref-K2_Koulibaly_86-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-K2_Koulibaly-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-giant_88-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-giant-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-gaffe_Deschamps_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gaffe_Deschamps-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> and <i>The Wall</i> from his fans.<sup id="cite_ref-scudetto_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scudetto-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In May 2019, it was announced that Koulibaly was named as an honorary citizen of <a href="/wiki/Naples" title="Naples">Naples</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> In April 2015, he was previously named as an honorary citizen of Saint-Dié-des-Vosges.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> He is so popular in Naples that an entrepreneur created a pizza after him and Koulibaly himself has spoken of his fondness for the city.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_BBC_Sport_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_BBC_Sport-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Koulibaly and his wife, Charline Oudenot, have a son together named Seni on 16 January 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> He became a second time father when his daughter Nessa was born on 28 August 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is a <a href="/wiki/Muslim" class="mw-redirect" title="Muslim">Muslim</a> and states that his name derived from the <a href="/wiki/Quran" title="Quran">Quran</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In addition to speaking French, Koulibaly also speaks English and Italian.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Throughout his time at Napoli, Koulibaly spoke out about <a href="/wiki/Racism_in_Italy" title="Racism in Italy">racism</a> in <a href="/wiki/Racism_in_association_football#Italy" title="Racism in association football">Italian football</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune_5-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Koulibaly_Players_Tribune-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In October 2019, Koulibaly called on the Italian football authorities to tackle racism by giving offenders a lifetime ban from entering the stadium.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> He had previously criticised the Italian football authorities for their lack of effort to tackle racism in January of that year.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalidou_Koulibaly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
